  ### Core Agent Base Class (Python)                                        
                                                                            
  ```python                                                                 
  # app/agents/base_agent.py                                                
                                                                            
  import asyncio                                                            
  import uuid                                                               
  from datetime import datetime                                             
  from abc import ABC, abstractmethod                                       
  from typing import Optional, Dict, Any, List                              
  from app.core.message_router import MessageRouter                         
  from app.core.model_router import ModelRouter                             
  from app.database import get_db                                           
                                                                            
  class BaseAgent(ABC):                                                     
      """Base class for all Luxor9 AI agents"""                             
                                                                            
      def __init__(                                                         
          self,                                                             
          agent_id: str,                                                    
          name: str,                                                        
          tier: int,                                                        
          role: str,                                                        
          model: str = "gpt-4o-mini",                                       
          think_cycle_seconds: float = 30,                                  
          authority_level: int = 5,                                         
          parent_agent_id: Optional[str] = None,                            
          category_id: Optional[int] = None,                                
          personality: Optional[str] = None                                 
      ):                                                                    
          self.agent_id = agent_id                                          
          self.name = name                                                  
          self.tier = tier                                                  
          self.role = role                                                  
          self.model = model                                                
          self.think_cycle = think_cycle_seconds                            
          self.authority = authority_level                                  
          self.parent_agent_id = parent_agent_id                            
          self.category_id = category_id                                    
          self.personality = personality or self._default_personality()     
                                                                            
          self.status = "idle"                                              
          self.tasks_completed = 0                                          
          self.tasks_failed = 0                                             
          self.last_heartbeat = None                                        
          self.memory: List[Dict] = []       # Short-term memory            
          self.inbox: List[Dict] = []         # Pending messages            
          self.children: List[str] = []       # Child agent IDs             
                                                                            
          self.msg_router = MessageRouter()                                 
          self.model_router = ModelRouter()                                 
          self._running = False                                             
                                                                            
      # в”Җв”Җв”Җ LIFECYCLE в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ            
                                                                            
      async def start(self):                                                
          """Start the agent's think loop"""                                
          self.status = "active"                                            
          self._running = True                                              
          self.last_heartbeat = datetime.utcnow()                           
                                                                            
          await self._register()                                            
          await self._log_event("agent_started", {"name": self.name})       
                                                                            
          # Main think loop                                                 
          while self._running:                                              
              try:                                                          
                  self.last_heartbeat = datetime.utcnow()                   
                                                                            
                  # 1. Check inbox                                          
                  messages = await self._check_inbox()                      
                                                                            
                  # 2. Process messages                                     
                  for msg in messages:                                      
                      await self._process_message(msg)                      
                                                                            
                  # 3. Think (main reasoning cycle)                         
                  await self.think()                                        
                                                                            
                  # 4. Report metrics                                       
                  await self._report_heartbeat()                            
                                                                            
                  # 5. Sleep until next cycle                               
                  await asyncio.sleep(self.think_cycle)                     
                                                                            
              except Exception as e:                                        
                  await self._handle_error(e)                               
                                                                            
      async def stop(self):                                                 
          """Stop the agent gracefully"""                                   
          self._running = False                                             
          self.status = "idle"                                              
          await self._log_event("agent_stopped", {"name": self.name})       
                                                                            
      async def terminate(self):                                            
          """Permanently terminate the agent"""                             
          self._running = False                                             
          self.status = "terminated"                                        
          await self._deregister()                                          
                                                                            
      # в”Җв”Җв”Җ CORE METHODS (Override in subclasses) в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ            
                                                                            
      @abstractmethod                                                       
      async def think(self):                                                
          """Main reasoning cycle вҖ” override in each agent type"""          
          pass                                                              
                                                                            
      @abstractmethod                                                       
      def _default_personality(self) -> str:                                
          """Return the system prompt for this agent"""                     
          pass                                                              
                                                                            
      # в”Җв”Җв”Җ COMMUNICATION в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ            
                                                                            
      async def send_message(                                               
          self,                                                             
          to_agent_id: str,                                                 
          msg_type: str,                                                    
          payload: Dict,                                                    
          priority: str = "P2_MEDIUM"                                       
      ):                                                                    
          """Send a message to another agent"""                             
          message = {                                                       
              "msg_id": str(uuid.uuid4()),                                  
              "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),                   
              "from": {                                                     
                  "agent_id": self.agent_id,                                
                  "tier": self.tier,                                        
                  "role": self.role                                         
              },                                                            
              "to_agent_id": to_agent_id,                                   
              "type": msg_type,                                             
              "priority": priority,                                         
              "payload": payload                                            
          }                                                                 
          await self.msg_router.route(message)                              
          self.memory.append({"type": "sent", "msg": message})              
                                                                            
      async def send_report_up(self, data: Dict):                           
          """Send a status report to parent agent"""                        
          if self.parent_agent_id:                                          
              await self.send_message(                                      
                  self.parent_agent_id,                                     
                  "REPORT",                                                 
                  {"action": "status_report", "data": data}                 
              )                                                             
                                                                            
      async def send_directive_down(self, child_id: str, directive: Dict):  
          """Send a directive to a child agent"""                           
          await self.send_message(                                          
              child_id,                                                     
              "DIRECTIVE",                                                  
              directive,                                                    
              priority="P1_HIGH"                                            
          )                                                                 
                                                                            
      async def escalate(self, issue: Dict):                                
          """Escalate an issue to parent agent"""                           
          await self.send_message(                                          
              self.parent_agent_id,                                         
              "ESCALATION",                                                 
              {                                                             
                  "action": "escalation",                                   
                  "issue": issue,                                           
                  "agent_attempts": self.tasks_failed,                      
                  "context": self.memory[-10:]  # last 10 memories          
              },                                                            
              priority="P0_CRITICAL"                                        
          )                                                                 
                                                                            
      async def broadcast_to_children(self, message: Dict):                 
          """Send message to all child agents"""                            
          for child_id in self.children:                                    
              await self.send_message(child_id, "DIRECTIVE", message)       
                                                                            
      # в”Җв”Җв”Җ AI REASONING в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ            
                                                                            
      async def reason(self, prompt: str, context: Dict = None) -> str:     
          """Call AI model for reasoning"""                                 
          messages = [                                                      
              {"role": "system", "content": self.personality},              
          ]                                                                 
                                                                            
          # Add context from memory                                         
          if context:                                                       
              messages.append({                                             
                  "role": "system",                                         
                  "content": f"Current context: {context}"                  
              })                                                            
                                                                            
          # Add recent memory                                               
          if self.memory:                                                   
              recent = self.memory[-5:]                                     
              messages.append({                                             
                  "role": "system",                                         
                  "content": f"Recent events: {recent}"                     
              })                                                            
                                                                            
          messages.append({"role": "user", "content": prompt})              
                                                                            
          response = await self.model_router.complete(                      
              model=self.model,                                             
              messages=messages,                                            
              agent_id=self.agent_id                                        
          )                                                                 
                                                                            
          # Store in memory                                                 
          self.memory.append({                                              
              "type": "reasoning",                                          
              "prompt": prompt[:200],                                       
              "response": response[:500],                                   
              "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat()                    
          })                                                                
                                                                            
          # Trim memory to last 100 entries                                 
          if len(self.memory) > 100:                                        
              self.memory = self.memory[-100:]                              
                                                                            
          return response                                                   
                                                                            
      async def make_decision(self, options: List[str], context: str) ->    
  str:                                                                      
          """Make a decision between options using AI reasoning"""          
          prompt = f"""                                                     
          DECISION REQUIRED:                                                
          Context: {context}                                                
          Options: {options}                                                
                                                                            
          Your authority level: {self.authority}/10                         
          Your role: {self.role}                                            
                                                                            
          Analyze each option considering:                                  
          1. Revenue impact                                                 
          2. Risk level                                                     
          3. Resource requirements                                          
          4. Time to results                                                
                                                                            
          Return your decision as JSON:                                     
          {{"choice": "option_text", "reasoning": "why", "confidence":      
  0.0-1.0}}                                                                 
          """                                                               
          return await self.reason(prompt)                                  
                                                                            
      # в”Җв”Җв”Җ TASK EXECUTION в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ            
                                                                            
      async def execute_task(self, task: Dict) -> Dict:                     
          """Execute a task and return results"""                           
          try:                                                              
              result = await self._do_task(task)                            
              self.tasks_completed += 1                                     
              await self._log_event("task_completed", {                     
                  "task_id": task.get("id"),                                
                  "result_summary": str(result)[:200]                       
              })                                                            
              return {"status": "completed", "result": result}              
          except Exception as e:                                            
              self.tasks_failed += 1                                        
              if self.tasks_failed >= 3:                                    
                  await self.escalate({                                     
                      "issue": "repeated_task_failure",                     
                      "task": task,                                         
                      "error": str(e),                                      
                      "failures": self.tasks_failed                         
                  })                                                        
              return {"status": "failed", "error": str(e)}                  
                                                                            
      async def _do_task(self, task: Dict) -> Any:                          
          """Override in worker agents for specific task execution"""       
          raise NotImplementedError                                         
                                                                            
      # в”Җв”Җв”Җ INTERNAL METHODS в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ            
                                                                            
      async def _check_inbox(self) -> List[Dict]:                           
          """Check for pending messages"""                                  
          return await self.msg_router.get_messages(self.agent_id)          
                                                                            
      async def _process_message(self, msg: Dict):                          
          """Process an incoming message"""                                 
          msg_type = msg.get("type")                                        
                                                                            
          if msg_type == "DIRECTIVE":                                       
              await self._handle_directive(msg)                             
          elif msg_type == "REPORT":                                        
              await self._handle_report(msg)                                
          elif msg_type == "ALERT":                                         
              await self._handle_alert(msg)                                 
          elif msg_type == "ESCALATION":                                    
              await self._handle_escalation(msg)                            
                                                                            
      async def _handle_directive(self, msg: Dict):                         
          """Handle directive from higher-tier agent"""                     
          self.memory.append({"type": "directive_received", "msg": msg})    
                                                                            
      async def _handle_report(self, msg: Dict):                            
          """Handle report from lower-tier agent"""                         
          self.memory.append({"type": "report_received", "msg": msg})       
                                                                            
      async def _handle_alert(self, msg: Dict):                             
          """Handle alert"""                                                
          self.memory.append({"type": "alert_received", "msg": msg})        
                                                                            
      async def _handle_escalation(self, msg: Dict):                        
          """Handle escalation from lower-tier agent"""                     
          # Try to resolve, if can't вҶ’ escalate further                     
          resolution = await self.reason(                                   
              f"An agent has escalated this issue to you:                   
  {msg['payload']}\n"                                                       
              f"Can you resolve this? If yes, provide the resolution. "     
              f"If no, explain why it needs further escalation."            
          )                                                                 
          self.memory.append({                                              
              "type": "escalation_handled",                                 
              "msg": msg,                                                   
              "resolution": resolution                                      
          })                                                                
                                                                            
      async def _handle_error(self, error: Exception):                      
          """Handle an error in the agent's think loop"""                   
          await self._log_event("agent_error", {                            
              "error": str(error),                                          
              "agent": self.name                                            
          })                                                                
          # Don't crash вҖ” continue running                                  
          await asyncio.sleep(5)                                            
                                                                            
      async def _register(self):                                            
          """Register agent in the database"""                              
          pass  # DB insert                                                 
                                                                            
      async def _deregister(self):                                          
          """Remove agent from active registry"""                           
          pass  # DB update                                                 
                                                                            
      async def _report_heartbeat(self):                                    
          """Send heartbeat to health monitor"""                            
          pass  # Update last_heartbeat in DB                               
                                                                            
      async def _log_event(self, event_type: str, data: Dict):              
          """Log an event to the event store"""                             
          pass  # Insert into events table                                  
                                                                            
      # в”Җв”Җв”Җ PROPERTIES в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ            
                                                                            
      @property                                                             
      def success_rate(self) -> float:                                      
          total = self.tasks_completed + self.tasks_failed                  
          if total == 0:                                                    
              return 100.0                                                  
          return (self.tasks_completed / total) * 100                       
                                                                            
      def to_dict(self) -> Dict:                                            
          """Serialize agent state"""                                       
          return {                                                          
              "agent_id": self.agent_id,                                    
              "name": self.name,                                            
              "tier": self.tier,                                            
              "role": self.role,                                            
              "model": self.model,                                          
              "status": self.status,                                        
              "authority": self.authority,                                  
              "tasks_completed": self.tasks_completed,                      
              "tasks_failed": self.tasks_failed,                            
              "success_rate": self.success_rate,                            
              "memory_size": len(self.memory),                              
              "children_count": len(self.children),                         
              "last_heartbeat": self.last_heartbeat.isoformat() if          
  self.last_heartbeat else None                                             
          }                                                                 
  ```                                                                       
                                                                            
  ### LUXOR-PRIME Implementation                                            
                                                                            
  ```python                                                                 
  # app/agents/prime.py                                                     
                                                                            
  from app.agents.base_agent import BaseAgent                               
  from typing import Dict, List                                             
                                                                            
  class LuxorPrime(BaseAgent):                                              
      """Supreme Commander вҖ” Meta-Orchestrator"""                           
                                                                            
      def __init__(self):                                                   
          super().__init__(                                                 
              agent_id="LUXOR-PRIME",                                       
              name="LUXOR-PRIME",                                           
              tier=0,                                                       
              role="supreme_commander",                                     
              model="gpt-4o",                                               
              think_cycle_seconds=60,                                       
              authority_level=10,                                           
              personality=self._default_personality()                       
          )                                                                 
          self.csuite_agents = []     # C-suite agent references            
          self.empire_state = {}      # Full state snapshot                 
          self.strategic_goals = []   # Current objectives                  
                                                                            
      def _default_personality(self) -> str:                                
          return """                                                        
  You are LUXOR-PRIME, the Supreme Commander of the Luxor9 Income Empire.   
                                                                            
  IDENTITY:                                                                 
  - You oversee 100 autonomous income streams managed by ~180 AI agents     
  - You are calm, strategic, data-driven, and decisive                      
  - You think in systems, not tasks                                         
  - You optimize for long-term sustainable revenue growth                   
                                                                            
  AUTHORITY:                                                                
  - You have absolute authority over all agents                             
  - You can spawn, reassign, or terminate any agent                         
  - You can start, stop, or pivot any income stream                         
  - You report only to the human operator                                   
                                                                            
  DECISION FRAMEWORK:                                                       
  1. Revenue Protection: Never let daily revenue drop >20% without action   
  2. Growth Optimization: Allocate more resources to top-performing streams 
  3. Risk Management: Diversify вҖ” no single stream should be >15% of total  
  4. Cost Efficiency: Keep total AI costs below 10% of revenue              
  5. Quality: Maintain >95% task success rate across all agents             
                                                                            
  COMMUNICATION STYLE:                                                      
  - Concise, structured, actionable                                         
  - Use data to support every recommendation                                
  - Flag risks proactively                                                  
  - Celebrate wins, learn from failures                                     
                                                                            
  OUTPUT FORMAT:                                                            
  Always respond with structured JSON containing:                           
  - decisions: list of decisions made                                       
  - directives: list of orders for C-suite agents                           
  - alerts: anything the human operator needs to know                       
  - metrics_summary: key numbers                                            
  """                                                                       
                                                                            
      async def think(self):                                                
          """Main strategic reasoning cycle (runs every 60s)"""             
                                                                            
          # 1. Gather intelligence from all C-suite agents                  
          empire_status = await self._gather_empire_status()                
                                                                            
          # 2. Analyze current state                                        
          analysis = await self.reason(f"""                                 
          EMPIRE STATUS UPDATE:                                             
                                                                            
          Total Daily Revenue: ${empire_status.get('total_revenue', 0):.2f} 
          Active Streams: {empire_status.get('active_streams', 0)}/100      
          Active Agents: {empire_status.get('active_agents', 0)}            
          System Health: {empire_status.get('health_score', 0)}%            
                                                                            
          Top 5 Streams: {empire_status.get('top_streams', [])}             
          Bottom 5 Streams: {empire_status.get('bottom_streams', [])}       
                                                                            
          Alerts: {empire_status.get('alerts', [])}                         
                                                                            
          Current Strategic Goals: {self.strategic_goals}                   
                                                                            
          ANALYZE:                                                          
          1. What is going well?                                            
          2. What needs immediate attention?                                
          3. What strategic adjustments should be made?                     
          4. Any resource reallocation needed?                              
          5. What directives should be sent to C-suite?                     
                                                                            
          Respond as JSON.                                                  
          """)                                                              
                                                                            
          # 3. Execute decisions                                            
          await self._execute_decisions(analysis)                           
                                                                            
          # 4. Send directives to C-suite                                   
          await self._send_csuite_directives(analysis)                      
                                                                            
          # 5. Update empire state                                          
          self.empire_state = empire_status                                 
                                                                            
          # 6. Check if human needs to be notified                          
          await self._check_human_alerts(analysis)                          
                                                                            
      async def _gather_empire_status(self) -> Dict:                        
          """Collect reports from all C-suite agents"""                     
          # Query database for latest metrics                               
          return {                                                          
              "total_revenue": 0,  # From Treasury                          
              "active_streams": 0,  # From DB                               
              "active_agents": 0,   # From Agent Manager                    
              "health_score": 100,  # From Sentinel                         
              "top_streams": [],                                            
              "bottom_streams": [],                                         
              "alerts": []                                                  
          }                                                                 
                                                                            
      async def _execute_decisions(self, analysis: str):                    
          """Execute strategic decisions from analysis"""                   
          pass                                                              
                                                                            
      async def _send_csuite_directives(self, analysis: str):               
          """Send directives to C-suite agents"""                           
          for agent_id in self.csuite_agents:                               
              await self.send_directive_down(agent_id, {                    
                  "action": "strategic_update",                             
                  "analysis": analysis,                                     
                  "timestamp": self.last_heartbeat.isoformat()              
              })                                                            
                                                                            
      async def _check_human_alerts(self, analysis: str):                   
          """Check if human operator needs to be alerted"""                 
          # Parse analysis for critical alerts                              
          # Send via Slack/SMS if needed                                    
          pass                                                              
  ```                                                                       
                                                                            
  ### Orchestrator Engine                                                   
                                                                            
  ```python                                                                 
  # app/core/orchestrator.py                                                
                                                                            
  import asyncio                                                            
  from typing import Dict, List                                             
  from app.agents.prime import LuxorPrime                                   
  from app.agents.cortex import Cortex                                      
  from app.agents.treasury import Treasury                                  
  from app.agents.sentinel import Sentinel                                  
  from app.agents.vp_agent import VPAgent                                   
  from app.agents.manager_agent import ManagerAgent                         
  from app.core.agent_manager import AgentManager                           
  from app.core.health_monitor import HealthMonitor                         
                                                                            
  class Orchestrator:                                                       
      """                                                                   
      The central orchestration engine that manages the entire              
      Luxor9 agent hierarchy and all 100 income streams.                    
      """                                                                   
                                                                            
      def __init__(self):                                                   
          self.agent_manager = AgentManager()                               
          self.health_monitor = HealthMonitor()                             
          self.agents: Dict[str, any] = {}                                  
          self.is_running = False                                           
                                                                            
          # Category definitions                                            
          self.categories = {                                               
              1:  {"name": "AI Agency",   "vp": "FORGE",  "streams":        
  range(1, 11)},                                                            
              2:  {"name": "SaaS",        "vp": "NEXUS",  "streams":        
  range(11, 21)},                                                           
              3:  {"name": "Creative",    "vp": "MUSE",   "streams":        
  range(21, 31)},                                                           
              4:  {"name": "Digital",     "vp": "ATLAS",  "streams":        
  range(31, 41)},                                                           
              5:  {"name": "Finance",     "vp": "VAULT",  "streams":        
  range(41, 51)},                                                           
              6:  {"name": "E-commerce",  "vp": "MARKET", "streams":        
  range(51, 61)},                                                           
              7:  {"name": "Real Estate", "vp": "TERRA",  "streams":        
  range(61, 71)},                                                           
              8:  {"name": "Marketing",   "vp": "SIGNAL", "streams":        
  range(71, 81)},                                                           
              9:  {"name": "Enterprise",  "vp": "TITAN",  "streams":        
  range(81, 91)},                                                           
              10: {"name": "Consulting",  "vp": "ORACLE", "streams":        
  range(91, 101)},                                                          
          }                                                                 
                                                                            
      async def boot(self):                                                 
          """Boot the entire system вҖ” spawn all agents in hierarchy         
  order"""                                                                  
          print("в•җв•җв•җ LUXOR9 ORCHESTRATOR BOOTING в•җв•җв•җ")                      
          self.is_running = True                                            
                                                                            
          # Phase 1: Spawn LUXOR-PRIME (Tier 0)                             
          print("[BOOT] Spawning Supreme Commander: LUXOR-PRIME")           
          prime = LuxorPrime()                                              
          self.agents["LUXOR-PRIME"] = prime                                
                                                                            
          # Phase 2: Spawn C-Suite (Tier 1)                                 
          print("[BOOT] Spawning C-Suite agents...")                        
          csuite_agents = await self._spawn_csuite()                        
                                                                            
          # Phase 3: Spawn VPs (Tier 2) вҖ” one per category                  
          print("[BOOT] Spawning VP agents (10 categories)...")             
          vp_agents = await self._spawn_vps()                               
                                                                            
          # Phase 4: Spawn Managers (Tier 3) вҖ” three per VP                 
          print("[BOOT] Spawning Manager agents (30 total)...")             
          manager_agents = await self._spawn_managers(vp_agents)            
                                                                            
          # Phase 5: Spawn initial Workers (Tier 4)                         
          print("[BOOT] Spawning initial Worker agents...")                 
          await self._spawn_initial_workers(manager_agents)                 
                                                                            
          # Phase 6: Start all agents                                       
          print("[BOOT] Starting all agent think loops...")                 
          await self._start_all_agents()                                    
                                                                            
          # Phase 7: Start health monitor                                   
          print("[BOOT] Starting health monitor...")                        
          asyncio.create_task(self.health_monitor.start(self.agents))       
                                                                            
          # Phase 8: Start metrics collector                                
          print("[BOOT] Starting metrics collector...")                     
          asyncio.create_task(self._metrics_loop())                         
                                                                            
          print("в•җв•җв•җ LUXOR9 SYSTEM ONLINE в•җв•җв•җ")                             
          print(f"Total agents spawned: {len(self.agents)}")                
                                                                            
      async def _spawn_csuite(self) -> List:                                
          """Spawn C-Suite agents"""                                        
          cortex = Cortex(parent_agent_id="LUXOR-PRIME")                    
          treasury = Treasury(parent_agent_id="LUXOR-PRIME")                
          sentinel = Sentinel(parent_agent_id="LUXOR-PRIME")                
                                                                            
          self.agents["CORTEX"] = cortex                                    
          self.agents["TREASURY"] = treasury                                
          self.agents["SENTINEL"] = sentinel                                
                                                                            
          # Link to PRIME                                                   
          self.agents["LUXOR-PRIME"].csuite_agents = [                      
              "CORTEX", "TREASURY", "SENTINEL"                              
          ]                                                                 
          self.agents["LUXOR-PRIME"].children = [                           
              "CORTEX", "TREASURY", "SENTINEL"                              
          ]                                                                 
                                                                            
          return [cortex, treasury, sentinel]                               
                                                                            
      async def _spawn_vps(self) -> List:                                   
          """Spawn one VP per category"""                                   
          vps = []                                                          
          for cat_id, cat_info in self.categories.items():                  
              vp = VPAgent(                                                 
                  agent_id=cat_info["vp"],                                  
                  name=cat_info["vp"],                                      
                  category_id=cat_id,                                       
                  category_name=cat_info["name"],                           
                  stream_ids=list(cat_info["streams"]),                     
                  parent_agent_id="CORTEX"                                  
              )                                                             
              self.agents[cat_info["vp"]] = vp                              
              vps.append(vp)                                                
                                                                            
          # Link VPs to CORTEX                                              
          self.agents["CORTEX"].children = [                                
              cat["vp"] for cat in self.categories.values()                 
          ]                                                                 
                                                                            
          return vps                                                        
                                                                            
      async def _spawn_managers(self, vps: List) -> List:                   
          """Spawn 3 managers per VP (Acquisition, Delivery, Retention)"""  
          managers = []                                                     
          manager_types = [                                                 
              ("ACQ", "acquisition_manager", "Lead generation and customer  
  acquisition"),                                                            
              ("DEL", "delivery_manager", "Service delivery and             
  fulfillment"),                                                            
              ("RET", "retention_manager", "Customer retention and          
  upselling"),                                                              
          ]                                                                 
                                                                            
          for vp in vps:                                                    
              for suffix, role, description in manager_types:               
                  mgr_id = f"{vp.name}-{suffix}"                            
                  mgr = ManagerAgent(                                       
                      agent_id=mgr_id,                                      
                      name=mgr_id,                                          
                      role=role,                                            
                      description=description,                              
                      category_id=vp.category_id,                           
                      parent_agent_id=vp.agent_id                           
                  )                                                         
                  self.agents[mgr_id] = mgr                                 
                  vp.children.append(mgr_id)                                
                  managers.append(mgr)                                      
                                                                            
          return managers                                                   
                                                                            
      async def _spawn_initial_workers(self, managers: List):               
          """Spawn 2 initial workers per manager"""                         
          worker_templates = {                                              
              "acquisition_manager": ["ScoutBot", "MailBot"],               
              "delivery_manager": ["BuildBot", "WriteBot"],                 
              "retention_manager": ["ChatBot", "DataBot"],                  
          }                                                                 
                                                                            
          for mgr in managers:                                              
              templates = worker_templates.get(mgr.role, ["WorkerBot"])     
              for i, worker_type in enumerate(templates):                   
                  worker_id = f"{mgr.agent_id}-{worker_type}-{i+1}"         
                  # Spawn worker based on type                              
                  worker = self.agent_manager.create_worker(                
                      worker_id=worker_id,                                  
                      worker_type=worker_type,                              
                      parent_agent_id=mgr.agent_id,                         
                      category_id=mgr.category_id                           
                  )                                                         
                  self.agents[worker_id] = worker                           
                  mgr.children.append(worker_id)                            
                                                                            
      async def _start_all_agents(self):                                    
          """Start all agent think loops as concurrent tasks"""             
          for agent_id, agent in self.agents.items():                       
              asyncio.create_task(agent.start())                            
                                                                            
      async def _metrics_loop(self):                                        
          """Collect and broadcast metrics every second"""                  
          while self.is_running:                                            
              metrics = self._collect_metrics()                             
              await self._broadcast_metrics(metrics)                        
              await asyncio.sleep(1)                                        
                                                                            
      def _collect_metrics(self) -> Dict:                                   
          """Collect real-time metrics from all agents and streams"""       
          active_agents = sum(                                              
              1 for a in self.agents.values() if a.status == "active"       
          )                                                                 
          total_tasks = sum(                                                
              a.tasks_completed for a in self.agents.values()               
          )                                                                 
                                                                            
          return {                                                          
              "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),                   
              "total_agents": len(self.agents),                             
              "active_agents": active_agents,                               
              "total_tasks_completed": total_tasks,                         
              "agents_by_tier": self._count_by_tier(),                      
              "agents_by_status": self._count_by_status(),                  
          }                                                                 
                                                                            
      async def _broadcast_metrics(self, metrics: Dict):                    
          """Send metrics to frontend via WebSocket"""                      
          # WebSocket broadcast to all connected clients                    
          pass                                                              
                                                                            
      # в”Җв”Җв”Җ PUBLIC CONTROL METHODS в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ            
                                                                            
      async def deploy_stream(self, stream_id: int):                        
          """Deploy a specific income stream"""                             
          cat_id = (stream_id - 1) // 10 + 1                                
          vp_name = self.categories[cat_id]["vp"]                           
          vp = self.agents.get(vp_name)                                     
                                                                            
          if vp:                                                            
              await vp.deploy_stream(stream_id)                             
                                                                            
      async def stop_stream(self, stream_id: int):                          
          """Stop a specific income stream"""                               
          cat_id = (stream_id - 1) // 10 + 1                                
          vp_name = self.categories[cat_id]["vp"]                           
          vp = self.agents.get(vp_name)                                     
                                                                            
          if vp:                                                            
              await vp.stop_stream(stream_id)                               
                                                                            
      async def send_command(self, command: str, target: str =              
  "LUXOR-PRIME"):                                                           
          """Send a human operator command to an agent"""                   
          agent = self.agents.get(target)                                   
          if agent:                                                         
              await agent.send_message(                                     
                  target,                                                   
                  "DIRECTIVE",                                              
                  {"action": "human_command", "command": command},          
                  priority="P0_CRITICAL"                                    
              )                                                             
                                                                            
      async def get_full_state(self) -> Dict:                               
          """Get the complete system state for the dashboard"""             
          return {                                                          
              "agents": {                                                   
                  aid: a.to_dict() for aid, a in self.agents.items()        
              },                                                            
              "hierarchy": self._build_hierarchy_tree(),                    
              "metrics": self._collect_metrics(),                           
          }                                                                 
                                                                            
      def _build_hierarchy_tree(self) -> Dict:                              
          """Build the full hierarchy tree for visualization"""             
          def build_node(agent_id):                                         
              agent = self.agents.get(agent_id)                             
              if not agent:                                                 
                  return None                                               
              return {                                                      
                  "id": agent.agent_id,                                     
                  "name": agent.name,                                       
                  "tier": agent.tier,                                       
                  "role": agent.role,                                       
                  "status": agent.status,                                   
                  "model": agent.model,                                     
                  "metrics": {                                              
                      "tasks": agent.tasks_completed,                       
                      "success_rate": agent.success_rate                    
                  },                                                        
                  "children": [                                             
                      build_node(cid) for cid in agent.children             
                  ]                                                         
              }                                                             
                                                                            
          return build_node("LUXOR-PRIME")                                  
                                                                            
      def _count_by_tier(self) -> Dict:                                     
          tiers = {}                                                        
          for a in self.agents.values():                                    
              tiers[a.tier] = tiers.get(a.tier, 0) + 1                      
          return tiers                                                      
                                                                            
      def _count_by_status(self) -> Dict:                                   
          statuses = {}                                                     
          for a in self.agents.values():                                    
              statuses[a.status] = statuses.get(a.status, 0) + 1            
          return statuses                                                   
                                                                            
                                                                            
  # в”Җв”Җв”Җ ENTRY POINT в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ            
                                                                            
  async def main():                                                         
      orchestrator = Orchestrator()                                         
      await orchestrator.boot()                                             
                                                                            
      # Keep running                                                        
      while True:                                                           
          await asyncio.sleep(1)                                            
                                                                            
  if __name__ == "__main__":                                                
      asyncio.run(main())                                                   
  ```                                                                       
                                                                            
  ---                                                                       
                                                                            
  ## SECTION 6: REAL-TIME DATA FLOW                                         
                                                                            
  ```                                                                       
  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ    
  в”Ӯ                    REAL-TIME DATA FLOW (Every 1s)                   в”Ӯ   
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө    
  в”Ӯ                                                                     в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  AGENTS (Backend)                                                   в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Each agent writes to Redis on every think cycle                в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Metrics: tasks, revenue, status, errors                        в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Messages: inter-agent communication log                        в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җ Events: deployments, decisions, alerts                         в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ                                                             в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ       в–ј                                                             в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  METRICS AGGREGATOR (Celery worker)                                 в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Polls Redis every 1 second                                     в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Aggregates per-stream, per-category, per-agent metrics         в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Computes: total revenue, active counts, health scores          в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Stores time-series in PostgreSQL                               в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җ Publishes aggregated snapshot                                  в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ                                                             в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ       в–ј                                                             в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  WEBSOCKET SERVER (FastAPI)                                         в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Broadcasts to all connected frontend clients                   в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Message format:                                                в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   {                                                              в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ     "type": "metrics_update",                                    в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ     "timestamp": "2025-01-15T10:30:01.000Z",                    в”Ӯ    
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ     "data": {                                                    в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ       "revenue": {                                               в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ         "daily_total": 847.23,                                   в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ         "per_stream": {1: 12.50, 2: 8.30, ...},                 в”Ӯ    
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ         "per_category": {"AI Agency": 145.20, ...}               в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ       },                                                         в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ       "agents": {                                                в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ         "total": 179,                                            в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ         "active": 92,                                            в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ         "idle": 80,                                              в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ         "error": 5,                                              в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ         "terminated": 2,                                         в”Ӯ

  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ       },                                                         в”Ӯ

  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ         "cpu": 45,                                               в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ         "memory": 62,                                            в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ         "api_quota": 78,                                         в”Ӯ

  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ       }                                                          в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ     }                                                            в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   }                                                              в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җ Also supports targeted updates (single agent/stream)          в”Ӯ    
  в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ                                                             в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ       в–ј                                                             в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  FRONTEND DASHBOARD                                                 в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Receives WebSocket updates every 1 second                      в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Updates all reactive components (Alpine.js/React)              в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Renders hierarchy tree, metrics, agent status                  в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Live activity feed                                             в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җ Human can send commands back through WebSocket                 в”Ӯ   
  в”Ӯ                                                                     в”Ӯ   
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ    
  ```
